				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					L'Office Catholique, Op.148 (Lefébure-Wély, Louis James Alfred)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>120 pieces divided in 10 suites
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1861-1862
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Versets&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Versets</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Communions&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Communions</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="15 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Masses&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Masses</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Marches&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Marches</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Benedictus&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Benedictus</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Fanfares&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Fanfares</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Preludes&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Preludes</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">L’Office Catholique
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">120 Morceaux divisés en dix Suites, composées pour l'harmonium ou l'orgue à tuyaux.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Lef%C3%A9bure-W%C3%A9ly,_Louis_James_Alfred" title="Category:Lefébure-Wély, Louis James Alfred">Lefébure-Wély, Louis James Alfred</a>
</td></tr>

<td>Op.148
</td></tr>

<td>ILL 49
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>120 pieces divided in 10 suites
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1861-1862
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
